### Output Format:
```
Output should be in Hindi Language only and must have following things.
1) Use the exact word which you found in your translation for each word in English sentence.
2) If there is no exact word available then you can use "क्रमांक" for number, "एंटर" for Enter, "परिणाम" for Result, "आइटम" for Item, "संख्या" for Number, "माफी" for Sorry, "अंतिम" for Last etc.
3) Please follow the grammar rules in hindi.
4) Please avoid using slangs or colloquial words.
5) Please write in the same order as it is in the input sentence.
6) Please do not add any punctuation marks in the output sentence.
7) Do not change the capitalization (uppercase/lowercase) of the words in the output sentence.
8) Do not translate the sentences literally.
9) The sentence should not contain more than 25 words.
```

[Hindi]: कोमल को अन्तिम समय में मुल्टिप्लेक्सी सरकारी अस्पताल, सेक्टर-१६ में ले जाकर उसे मृत्यु पहुंचा दिया गया।

*/

class Translate {
    static int count = 0;
    
    public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException {
        BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        
        String inputLine = null;
        do {
            System.out.println("Enter an English Sentence and its Hindi Translation");
            
            // Get input line
            inputLine = br.readLine();
            
            if (inputLine == null || inputLine.isEmpty()) {
                break;
            }
            
            // Check if there is any newline character present in the string
            if (inputLine.contains("\n")) {
                System.out.println("Please enter only one sentence at a time.");
                continue;
            }
            
            String english = inputLine.split("\\s+")[0];
            String hindi = translate(english);
            
            System.out.print("Translation : ");
            System.out.println(hindi);
            
            count++;
        } while (true);
        
        System.out.println("Total number of sentences translated : " + count);
    }
    
    private static String translate(String sentence) {
        String result = "";
        for (int i = 0; i < sentence.length() - 1; i++) {
            char c = sentence.charAt(i);
            if (Character.isUpperCase(c)) {
                c = Character.toLowerCase(c);
            }
            result += c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}</s>

#### Part - II

In this part you will be given an English Sentence and asked to find out the Hindi word which can be used to translate it into Hindi. You need to write down the correct Hindi word in the space provided.

Example:
[English]: The company has appointed a new managing director who has worked with many top companies in India and abroad. 
[Hindi]: यह कंपनी एक नए अध्यक्ष नियुक्त कर दिया है जो भारत और विदेश में कई ऊँची प्रतिनिधित्व कंपनियों में काम कर चुके हैं।
                                                                          
The answer for the example above is :
[Hindi]: अध्यक्ष

[Hindi]: अंत तक किस तरह का है

Input Format: First line contains the Sentence in English and second line contains the Sentence in Hindi.  
Output Format: Output will be in Hindi as per the input format.
"""
import re
from collections import Counter


def main():
    f = open("data.txt", "r")
    lines = f.readlines()
    for i in range(len(lines)):
        words_in_sentence = []
        hindi_words = []
        english_words = []
        for j in range(i + 1):
            if (j == len(lines) - 1):
                break
            line = lines[j].strip().split(' ')
            for k in range(len(line)):
                if line[k] not in words_in_sentence:
                    words_in_sentence.append(line[k])
        for word in words_in_sentence:
            hindi_word = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]+', '', word).lower()
            hindi_words.append(hindi_word)
        for word in hindi_words:
            if word in english_words:
                continue
            else:
                english_words.append(word)
        hindi_sentence = ' '.join(hindi_words)
        english_sentence = ' '.join(english_words)
        print(hindi_sentence, english_sentence)
    f.close()


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
</s>
[Actual Hindi]: यानि कि आवेदन के सात दिन के भीतर डीटीओ ऑफिस को डीएल तैयार करके आवेदक को देना होगा।

1) पिछले (last year) should be पिछले साल (last year). 
2) कुछ जगहों (some places) should be कुछ जगहों पर (at some places).
3) दिवाली (Diwali) should be दिवाली पर (on Diwali).
4) में (in) should be में पर (at).
5) गई (conducted) should be गई जांच में (during the investigation).
6) ध्वनि (noise) should be ध्वनि प्रदूषण (noise pollution).
7) तक (reached) should be था (was).
8) में (in) should be में तक (up to).
9) प्रदूषण (pollution) should be प्रदूषण तक (pollution up to).
10) १०० (one hundred) should be १०० डेसीबल (one hundred decibels).

### [Part - 4](https://github.com/pranav9876/Coding-Interview-Preparation/tree/master/Questions/English%20to%20Hindi) - Questions related to English to Hindi and vice versa.

#### Exercise - 1:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the first string is palindrome else false. For example, 'Madam' -> true, 'mom' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isPalindrome(string s){
    int len = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<len/2;i++){
        if (s[i] != s[len-1-i]){
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}
```

#### Exercise - 2:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the second string is a permutation of the first string else false. For example, 'ABC' -> true, 'ABD' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isPermutation(string s, string t){
    int n = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if (t[i] != s[i]){
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}
```

#### Exercise - 3:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the first string is subsequence of the second string else false. For example, 'abcd' -> true, 'abcde' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isSubSequence(string s, string t){
    int n = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if (t.
[Actual Hindi]: सामान्य दिनों में यह आंकड़ा ५५ डेसीबल होता है।

### Part 3 - Spell Checker

Spelling is an important aspect for a translator as well. So we have provided a spell checker too which will help you in identifying your spelling mistakes and correct it on the spot.

### Part 4 - Grammar Checker

Grammar is another important aspect of translation. This part helps you identify any grammatical error or punctuation mistake that might be there in your text.

### Part 5 - Word Frequency Analyzer

Word frequency analyser gives you the frequency of words used in the text so that you can understand the frequency of each word in the text.

### Part 6 - Sentence Completion

Sentence completion is one of the most useful tools for a translator. This tool provides you with suggestions of what you should write next after typing some text.

### Part 7 - Auto-suggest

Auto-suggest is a very useful feature for translators who translate sentences or paragraphs repeatedly. It saves a lot of time for such users.

### Part 8 - Text To Speech (TTS)

Text to speech feature allows you to listen to the translated text spoken aloud. This is helpful if you want to test the pronunciation of a word or phrase.

### Part 9 - OCR

OCR stands for Optical Character Recognition. This feature extracts characters from an image or scanned document and converts it into editable text.

### Part 10 - TTS & OCR

This is a combination of both TTS and OCR features. You can use this feature to listen to the text spoken out loud and then convert it into editable

### Part - 4 : Grammar Rules (5 Marks)

Write the rules for the following sentences:
(i) The word 'but' is used to connect two negative sentences.

(ii) The verb 'to be' can also be used as an auxiliary verb.

(iii) In indirect speech, we use 'said' after reporting verbs like tell, ask etc.

(iv) The past participle form of the verb 'be' is 'been'.

(v) When the subject is 'I', 'you' or 'we', the present tense form of 'have' is 'has'.

(vi) 'A few' means 'not many'.

(vii) We do not use articles before names of languages.

(viii) A preposition can be followed by either a noun or a pronoun.

(ix) 'Nevertheless' is used when you want to say that something has happened despite the fact that it should not have happened.

(x) The adverb 'already' indicates time.

(xi) The verb 'can' is used to express possibility.

(xii) An infinitive is a verb without 'to' in front of it.

(xiii) A gerund is formed by adding '-ing' to the base form of a verb.

(xiv) The phrase 'it was' is used to introduce a statement which took place earlier than the main clause.

(xv) A noun phrase consists of a noun and
[Actual Hindi]: परिवार में दो बेटे और तीन बेटियां हैं।

//Function to convert string into uppercase and lowercase.
string ToUpper(string str) {
    if (str == null || str.Length < 1) return "";
    StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
    for (int i = 0; i < str.Length; i++) {
        char c = str[i];
        if (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z')
            c -= ('a'-'A');
        else if (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z')
            c += ('a'-'A');
        sb.Append((char)c);
    }
    return sb.ToString();
}

{
    static void Main()
    {
        string inputStr = Console.ReadLine();
        string[] words = inputStr.Split(' ');
        Dictionary<string, int>

#### 5.13.2) [Bonus] 100% Correctness Tests

In this section you will be provided with some sentences which have been translated incorrectly and your job would be to correct those sentences.

Example 1:
[English]: It was reported that there were more than two hundred people killed in an accident near Agra yesterday.
[Hindi]: आगरा के आज के साथ और पांच हज़ार लोगों की मौत दर्शाई गई।

Solution:
It should be "There were more than two thousand people killed..." instead of "more than five thousand".

Example 2:
[English]: The investigation revealed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
[Hindi]: जांच में पता चला कि ध्वनि प्रदूषण १०० डेसीबल तक पहुँचा गया।

Solution:
The correct translation for the sentence above should be: "The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels."

Example 3:
[English]: There were more than two thousand people killed in an accident near Agra yesterday.
[Hindi]: आगरा के आज के साथ और पांच हज़ार लोगों की मौत दर्शाई गई।

Solution:
This sentence should
[Actual Hindi]: मथुरा वासियों को कंस के अत्याचारों से मुक्ति दिलाने के लिए भगवान कृष्ण ने जन्म लिया था।

### Question 2:
Write a Python program to check whether a given number is even or odd?
```python
def is_even(num):
    if num % 2 == 0:
        return True
    else:
        return False

print("is_even(5) = ", is_even(5))
```

### Question 3:
Write a Python program to find the sum of all even numbers between 1 and 100?
```python
def sum_of_even(n):
    s = 0
    for i in range(1, n+1):
        if i%2==0:
            s+=i
    return s

print(sum_of_even(100))
```

### Question 4:
Write a Python program to check if a string is palindrome or not?
```python
def is_palindrome(s):
    if len(s) < 2:
        return True
    
    first = s[0]
    last = s[-1]
    
    if first != last:
        return False
    
    mid = len(s)/2 - 1
    for i in range(mid,-1,-1):
        if s[i] != s[len(s)-i-1]:
            return False
        
    return True

print(is_palindrome('abcd'))
```

### Part B:
This part will test your understanding of grammar rules and their application. 
There will be two questions which you need to answer with correct answers.

#### Question 1:
Write the sentences in English and then translate it into Hindi using the following rule:
- Subject + Verb + Object (SVO)
- Direct object comes before Indirect object
- If there is no direct object, use "to" instead of "for" or "in"
- If there is no indirect object, use "for" or "in" instead of "to"
- "For" should not be used for animals
- In case of multiple objects, use "of" between each one

**Example 1:**
[English]: I gave him a book for his birthday.
[Hindi]: मैं उसे उसकी जन्मदिन पर किताब दे दिया।

**Example 2:**
[English]: She gave her daughter a doll for Christmas.
[Hindi]: उसने उसे उसकी दूसरी दिन पर खिल्ला दे दिया।

**Example 3:**
[English]: He bought me a dress for my birthday.
[Hindi]: उसने मेरे जन्मदिन पर मेरे लिए एक सूट ख़रीदा।

**Example 4:**
[English]: I gave him some flowers for his birthday.
[Hindi]: मैं �
[Actual Hindi]: इस अवसर पर बाल कृष्ण ठाकुर, रमेशचंद ठाकुर, उमादत्त गौतम व रमेश ठाकुर आदि मौजूद रहे।
==================================================

Following the same format above from the examples, What is the Translation of the sentence given below. 
[English]: Avni is from the Gandhinagar district of Gujrat. 
[Hindi]: अवनी गांधीनगर जिले की आदित्य हैं।
                                                                                                           

*/
class Solution {
    public String translate(String s) {
        char[] ch = s.toCharArray();
        
        int i=0;
        int j=ch.length-1;
        
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        
        while (i<j){
            
            if (Character.isUpperCase(ch[i])){
                sb.append(' ');
                i++;
            }else{
                sb.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch[i]));
                i++;
            }
            
            if (Character.isUpperCase(ch[j])){
                sb.append(' ');
                j--;
            }else{
                sb.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch[j]));
                j--;
            }
            
        }
        
        return sb.toString();
    }
}</s>

### 10. [Linguistic Requirements for the Language:](https://github.com/sid-kumar/Lexical-Similarity-Analysis/blob/master/Language%20Requirement.md)
The following are the linguistic requirements for the language. Please check your language if it meets all these requirements. If not, then you can still participate but your project might be rejected. 
1. 256 character limit for each word (inclusive of spaces).
2. No punctuation marks except spaces.
3. Words should start with a capital letter and end with a full stop.
4. Words must have a minimum of two characters.
5. Words should not contain numbers or special symbols like $, @ etc.
6. Words must be in lower case letters.
7. Words must not contain more than one space between them.
8. Each word must have exactly one meaning.
9. Word forms should be in their standard form (e.g., 'dogs' instead of 'dog').
10. Words must be written in alphabetical order.

### 11. [Data Requirements for the Language:](https://github.com/sid-kumar/Lexical-Similarity-Analysis/blob/master/Data%20Requirements.md)
The following are the data requirements for the language. Please check your language if it meets all these requirements. If not, then you can still participate but your project might be rejected. 
1. At least 500 words for training and testing.
2. At least 1000 sentences per document.
3. Sentences should be in English and translated into the target language.
4. The data should be split into training and test sets.
5. The dataset should include both the original and the translation versions of the documents.
6. Documents should be written in a clear and concise manner.
7. The data should be well-formatted and easy

[Hindi]: एंजली अभी भी उतरी हुई थी।

*/

class Solution {
    public String translate(String s) {
        // Write your code here
        String[] arr = s.split(" ");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        
        for (int i=0;i<arr.length-1;i++) {
            if (i == 0 || i == arr.length - 1){
                sb.append(arr[i]).append(" ");
            } else {
                sb.append(arr[i]).append(" के लिए ");
            }
            
            sb.append(arr[i+1]);
        }
        
        return sb.toString().trim();
    }
}</s>
[Actual Hindi]: तब तक अंजली भी आ गई।

###### Solution:
The following steps can be used for this problem:
* Read the input string carefully.
* Find out the position of 'in', which should come after 'the'.
* Find the position of 'of' which comes after 'the'.
* Count the number of words between 'in' and 'of'.
* Now find the next word after 'of'. This will be the first word in the sentence.
* Then count the number of words between the first word and 'and'.
* Finally count the number of words between 'and' and 'police'.

def translate(input_string):
    # Your code here
    return input_string

"""

import argparse
import os
import sys
from typing import List

sys.path.append("../")

from translator_main import translate_english_to_hindi


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument(
        "--input", type=str, default="data/example.txt", help="Input file path"
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--output", type=str, default="data/output.txt", help="Output file path"
    )
    args = parser.parse_args()

    if not os.path.isfile(args.input):
        print("Input file {} does not exist!".format(args.input))
        return -1

    sentences = []
    with open(args.input) as f:
        for line in f:
            sentences.append(line.strip())

    translated_sentences = translate_english_to_hindi(sentences)

    with open(args.output, "w+") as f:
        for i, sent in enumerate(translated_sentences):
            f.write(f"{i}. {sent}\n")

    print("Done!")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

##### 4. Hindi Grammar for Class X

The grammar portion is very easy to understand as it has only few rules which you need to follow. Here we have mentioned some important points regarding this topic. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X contains only few rules so its easier to remember. 
* There are many ways to write a word in hindi. 
* There are some rules regarding the usage of words like "Dhan" , "Ghar" etc. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X has only 5 parts of speech i.e. Nouns, Pronouns, Verbs, Adjectives and Adverbs. 
* There are some special rules for writing numbers in hindi like "Khata" , "Tola" etc. 
* Some words in hindi are used in plural form. 
* There are some special words in hindi which are used in both singular and plural forms. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X also includes the use of punctuation marks. 

##### 5. Vocabulary

Vocabulary section is very important part of SSC CGL examination because it will help you to score maximum marks in this paper. There are around 300 questions in vocabulary section which is equal to 100 marks. This means if you know the meaning of each word then you can easily attempt all these questions without any difficulty.

You should focus on following things related to Vocabulary Section:
* Read Newspapers daily to increase your vocabulary power.
* Read the book named "Word Power Made Easy".

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;
class Test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        //your code here
        Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
        String str="";
        int i=0;
        System.out.println("Enter your text");
        str=sc.nextLine();
        for (i = 0; i < str.length(); i++)
        {
            if((str.charAt(i)>='a' && str.charAt(i)<='z')||(str.charAt(i)>='A' && str.charAt(i)<='Z'))
                System.out.print((char)(str.charAt(i)+32));
            else
                System.out.print((char)(str.charAt(i)));
        }
    }
}</s>

First line contains T, number of test cases (T<=10). Then for each test case it has two lines. First line contains N, total number of sentences(N>=1) and second line contains N sentences.

Each sentence is made up of maximum 50 words. Each word can contain alphabets and digits from 'a' to 'z', 'A' to 'Z'.

7

सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।
आज से बाद में विवाद किया जा सकता है।
